  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_245e325f-9a51-40a7-9010-dc6e7f6e65ad'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();

  <span id="freeText10272186720238329308" style="display:none"><i>Your Escape Into A World of Dark Mysteries &amp; Spicy Romance.</i><br /><br />After being left at the altar, Jade Roberts seeks solace at her best friend’s ranch on the Colorado western slope. Her humiliation still ripe, she doesn't expect to be attracted to her friend’s reticent brother, but when the gorgeous cowboy kisses her, all bets are off.<br /><br />Talon Steel is broken. Having never fully healed from a horrific childhood trauma, he simply exists, taking from women what is offered and giving nothing in return...until Jade Roberts catapults into his life. She is beautiful, sweet, and giving, and his desire for her becomes a craving he fears he'll never be able to satisfy.<br /><br />Passion sizzles between the two lovers...but long-buried secrets haunt them both and may eventually tear them apart.</span>

If the book was more complete and some situation<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">The main characters basically focused on their sexual attractions that never really were interesting. If the book was more complete and some situations resolved it may have been interesting. Amazon may have read the following books but I felt that this book didn't end very well or spurn my interest to read the following series.<br /> <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

    <div class="section firstReview">
      

<div id="review_1608865205" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1608865205" />
    <a title="Jessica Ann" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22722176-jessica-ann"><img alt="Jessica Ann" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1538579265p2/22722176.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1608865205?book_show_action=true">Apr 12, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica Ann" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica Ann" href="/user/show/22722176-jessica-ann">Jessica Ann</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781943893171" href="/book/show/27819474-craving">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1608865205" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14873928050404958133">An seat gripping, emotional masterpiece!<br/><br/>Helen has stolen my heart with this epic story of 2 broken souls. I opened this ARC with the intention of it lasting a couple of evenings of after work reading. Wow was I wrong, I started and finished this book in 4 hours. I didn't even stop for a break, I couldn't. I was drawn in from the very first chapter. I can not wait for more of the Steel Brothers. <br/><br/>I was blown away with the story that is Talon and Jade. They both have walls built, they both have bee</span>
  <span id="freeText14873928050404958133" style="display:none">An seat gripping, emotional masterpiece!<br /><br />Helen has stolen my heart with this epic story of 2 broken souls. I opened this ARC with the intention of it lasting a couple of evenings of after work reading. Wow was I wrong, I started and finished this book in 4 hours. I didn't even stop for a break, I couldn't. I was drawn in from the very first chapter. I can not wait for more of the Steel Brothers. <br /><br />I was blown away with the story that is Talon and Jade. They both have walls built, they both have been hurt and humiliated, one much more than the other, but they have protected their hearts to not fall in love. But will their emotions get the best of them? <br /><br />Jade has just been left at the alter and decided to move in with her best friend on the Steel ranch, when she gets to the airport Marj (Jade's best friend) was not able to pick her up so she sent her brother Talon. The one Steel brother she hasn't meet. And the chemistry she felt was instant, but she was determined to not let him get to her. <br /><br />Talon has served in the military and seen things he wish he hadn't. He also suffers from what appears to be a childhood trauma. He has been severely hurt and doesn't know how to show any emotion other than he is a master in the bedroom (His words, not mine.) He is the perfect Alpha Male; tall, dark, and extremely sexy. But his emotional walls are taller than the wall in China. He knows he has feelings for Jade, or at least he thinks he does. Will the 2 ever really be able to open up to one another? Oh I wish I knew. </span>
  <a data-text-id="14873928050404958133" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer2257477597253635891"><strong>The angst is so frustrating it’s perfect!</strong><br/><br/>This is my first Helen Hardt book and I LOVED IT!! I didn’t expect it to go so deep just from the description but Jade and Talon take you down quite a rabbit hole that leaves you wanting more and dying for the next book!<br/><br/>Poor sweet Jade has just been left at the alter after seven years with her boyfriend turned fiancé. With no where to go, she moves in with her college roommate while she rebuilds her life and wait for the result from her bar exam. Talon is</span>
  <span id="freeText2257477597253635891" style="display:none"><strong>The angst is so frustrating it’s perfect!</strong><br /><br />This is my first Helen Hardt book and I LOVED IT!! I didn’t expect it to go so deep just from the description but Jade and Talon take you down quite a rabbit hole that leaves you wanting more and dying for the next book!<br /><br />Poor sweet Jade has just been left at the alter after seven years with her boyfriend turned fiancé. With no where to go, she moves in with her college roommate while she rebuilds her life and wait for the result from her bar exam. Talon is her best friend’s brother and as soon as she lays eyes on him she instantly attracted. He feels exactly the same way, but his dark and troubled past won’t allow him to let anyone in, not even his family, and certainly Jade. <br /><br />The push and pull of this book is FANTASTIC! Just when you think Jade is working her way in even so slightly, Talon pushes her away. But he wants her so bad!! He wars with himself, desperately wanting her but refusing to hurt her by being with him. It’s deliciously maddening!!<br /><br />I thoroughly enjoyed this book and can’t wait to read the next one! Talon is so beautifully broken he makes the perfect book boyfriend that you just want to love and heal. And Jade and Talon are so HOT together! Excellent read!</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1920470627" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16442054635966856010">Craving 'Craving' by Helen Hardt is book One in the "Steel Brothers" Saga. This is the story of Talon and Jade. There is a cliffhanger to this book so please make note of that. I will say that even though I am not a fan of cliffhangers I understand how much another book was needed when dealing with Talon and Jade's story. In addition, please note I thought this was shadowing on a Dark Romance type theme. Not so much heart and flowers of traditional romances. Jade is uprooting herself from her ho</span>
  <span id="freeText16442054635966856010" style="display:none">Craving 'Craving' by Helen Hardt is book One in the "Steel Brothers" Saga. This is the story of Talon and Jade. There is a cliffhanger to this book so please make note of that. I will say that even though I am not a fan of cliffhangers I understand how much another book was needed when dealing with Talon and Jade's story. In addition, please note I thought this was shadowing on a Dark Romance type theme. Not so much heart and flowers of traditional romances. Jade is uprooting herself from her hometown after being left at the alter. Her best friend Marjorie talks her into coming to stay with her and look for a job there. So Jade heads out to make a new start!Marjorie’s brother Talon picks her up at the airport. This is the first time Jade has met Talon and she is shocked by her reaction. Jade is quickly hot for him but he is not a talkative person and seems distant. Not like his brothers and sister. Talon too can't believe how much he wants Jade but he has a mind set not to get close to any women...and just take what they willing give. But that is hard to stick to around Jade...but he does tries to keep a distance. It didn't take long to fall in love with this story! <div id="review_1710847898" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1710847898" />
    <a title="Elle&#39;s Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44344367-elle-s-book-blog"><img alt="Elle&#39;s Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1601066023p2/44344367.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1710847898?book_show_action=true">Jul 27, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elle&#39;s Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elle&#39;s Book Blog" href="/user/show/44344367-elle-s-book-blog">Elle&#39;s Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781943893171" href="/book/show/27819474-craving">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44344367-elle-s-book-blog?shelf=top-favorites">top-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44344367-elle-s-book-blog?shelf=series-first-fav">series-first-fav</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44344367-elle-s-book-blog?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44344367-elle-s-book-blog?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1710847898" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2678337593044738807"><b> Genre: </b> Contemporary Romance<br/><b> Release Date: </b> May 3, 2016<br/><b> Cliffhanger: </b> Yes. But book 2 is available now!<br/><br/><b> :: 5 Pretty Little Stars :: </b><br/><br/>WOAH. I didn’t expect to love this book as much as I did. After all, it does end in the dreaded cliffhanger that many readers are opposed to. And in all honesty, I wasn’t sure what to expect because I haven’t read any of the authors previous books. However, this one totally ignited a flame inside me and tore me to SHREDS. It’s emotional (there are hints of sexual a</span>
  <span id="freeText2678337593044738807" style="display:none"><b> Genre: </b> Contemporary Romance<br /><b> Release Date: </b> May 3, 2016<br /><b> Cliffhanger: </b> Yes. But book 2 is available now!<br /><br /><b> :: 5 Pretty Little Stars :: </b><br /><br />WOAH. I didn’t expect to love this book as much as I did. After all, it does end in the dreaded cliffhanger that many readers are opposed to. And in all honesty, I wasn’t sure what to expect because I haven’t read any of the authors previous books. However, this one totally ignited a flame inside me and tore me to SHREDS. It’s emotional (there are hints of sexual abuse), it’s angsty, and it downright pulls at every inch of your heart. It didn’t matter to me that it ended in a cliffy because it was that good. Plus, it helps that book two is not available! Anyway, I would certainly recommend this one. It’s pretty heartbreaking when you take in the whole story but I am hoping that once the story is finished (in book 3) that we will find that just because someone is broken doesn’t mean they can’t be fixed. I am totally crossing my fingers for Talon because I fell head over heels in love with him… <br /><br />So, this book is about a broken man and a woman that would do anything to fix him. The problem though is that Talon (the stories hero) doesn’t want someone to fix him. He is seemingly content to stay on his own and live his existence in solitude. This is what his initial reaction is anyway. But for some reason, he can’t seem to stay away from Jade…<br /><br />Jade is Talon’s sisters best friend. And after being left at the alter by her (now) ex fiancé, she needs and escape and going to friends small town home seems like the best option for her. When she first meets Talon she knows she is in for trouble. This man is the quiet and brooding kind, and getting close to him is difficult at best. But the two have a lot of chemistry even though they both deny it, at first… <br /><br />Both Jade and Talon will quickly steal reader’s hearts. The connection, the angst, and the overall vulnerability of the characters is quite beautiful. But buried secrets and harsh realities that test this couple will leave readers gripping the edge of their books and hoping and praying for a miracle for these two. So, if you love a book that will take you on a tough journey with the characters than I strongly suggest picking this one up. Right when I was finished I bought book 2 and book 3 will be out in September (I can’t wait). With all this being said, I will seriously be looking into more of the authors work. </span>
  <a data-text-id="2678337593044738807" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Kristin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10957272-kristin"><img alt="Kristin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1342582232p2/10957272.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1615483651?book_show_action=true">Apr 19, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin" href="/user/show/10957272-kristin">Kristin</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781943893171" href="/book/show/27819474-craving">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1615483651" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3125421930761667483">This was my first book by Helen Hardt and it will not be my last. This story of a man- Talon Steel- with a tortured soul trying to find his way back to the living after Jade Roberts comes colliding into his life. Jade - fresh from disaster that is her love life- takes the offer of a place for a fresh start from her best friend, Marj Steel. The tension and sparks are there from the moment that Talon and Jade met and just get stronger as time goes on. However, Talon cant let got of his past so he </span>
  <span id="freeText3125421930761667483" style="display:none">This was my first book by Helen Hardt and it will not be my last. This story of a man- Talon Steel- with a tortured soul trying to find his way back to the living after Jade Roberts comes colliding into his life. Jade - fresh from disaster that is her love life- takes the offer of a place for a fresh start from her best friend, Marj Steel. The tension and sparks are there from the moment that Talon and Jade met and just get stronger as time goes on. However, Talon cant let got of his past so he is hot one minute and freezing Jade out the next. I love that Jade is written as a strong women who has decided not to give up. The intense emotion in this book really kept me from putting it down. The book does end in a cliffhanger that left me immediately looking up when the next book was due out - which thankfully was not long from now. Can not wait to read Obsession. I really expect the entire Steel family series to become a favorite of mine . </span>
  <a data-text-id="3125421930761667483" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1618062827" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1618062827" />
    <a title="Celina Summers" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5139371-celina-summers"><img alt="Celina Summers" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1461382071p2/5139371.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1618062827?book_show_action=true">Apr 22, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Celina Summers" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Celina Summers" href="/user/show/5139371-celina-summers">Celina Summers</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781943893171" href="/book/show/27819474-craving">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1618062827" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13307002483942331082">This isn't your everyday erotic romance. Helen Hardt has created deeply flawed characters with recognizable demons, and turned them into masterpieces of character development. Although the erotic elements are...well...uber HOT, they are not the heart and soul of this story. What this book lives and dies on is the relationship between Jade, who just suffered the humiliation of being left at the altar, and Talon, a man whose tortured past exceeds anything you could possibly imagine. What makes the</span>
  <span id="freeText13307002483942331082" style="display:none">This isn't your everyday erotic romance. Helen Hardt has created deeply flawed characters with recognizable demons, and turned them into masterpieces of character development. Although the erotic elements are...well...uber HOT, they are not the heart and soul of this story. What this book lives and dies on is the relationship between Jade, who just suffered the humiliation of being left at the altar, and Talon, a man whose tortured past exceeds anything you could possibly imagine. What makes the story--and the relationship--work is the incredible development of these two characters who do not resemble any I've seen in erotic romance--and as I've been an editor for over a decade and have worked with some of the top erotic romance authors in the world, that's saying a lot. You may buy this book for the sexual elements, but you'll fall in love with this book for the story. Hardt treats sensitive emotional issues with compassion--and that compassion is ultimately what fuels the plot. This is the most original, most gut-wrenching, and most incredible erotic romance I've ever put my hands on. When you read this book, you'll fall in love with it too--and rejoice that there are eight more books in the Steel Brothers Saga. Craving is a must-read novel for 2016. Bravo.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13307002483942331082" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2373592961" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2373592961" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2373592961?book_show_action=true">Apr 26, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="TheSassyNerdBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="TheSassyNerdBlog" href="/user/show/81294015-thesassynerdblog">TheSassyNerdBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2373592961" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5374710573342658562">How can I put into words just how amazing this book is? Craving is book 1 in the Steel Brothers series and it focuses on the Steel family. Book 1 is the start of Talon and Jade's intense, beautiful, broken, addictive, gut-wrenching, heartbreaking, and all-consuming love story.<br/><br/>I'll admit, at first I struggled to get into this, not much but enough to think "Well maybe this isn't for me"... Oh, how wrong was I? I am so so so glad I kept reading. At that moment, I thanked myself for being stubborn. </span>
  <span id="freeText5374710573342658562" style="display:none">How can I put into words just how amazing this book is? Craving is book 1 in the Steel Brothers series and it focuses on the Steel family. Book 1 is the start of Talon and Jade's intense, beautiful, broken, addictive, gut-wrenching, heartbreaking, and all-consuming love story.<br><br>I'll admit, at first I struggled to get into this, not much but enough to think "Well maybe this isn't for me"... Oh, how wrong was I? I am so so so glad I kept reading. At that moment, I thanked myself for being stubborn. By the 1/4 of the way through the book, I was hooked! Completely obsessed and I needed to know what happened, what was happening and what this author had in store for us readers. And she did not disappoint. Book 1 is only the beginning and let me tell you now, it is one hell of a beginning! You will be hooked, you will be intrigued, you will be obsessed and you will crave more.<br><br>Talon is a man with demons, with a dark, sordid, disturbing, torturous past that he struggles daily with. After going through a horrid and traumatic experience when he was just a boy, it has left him broken beyond belief. Demons taking over his life, his love life and his relationships with his family.<br><br>Jade was strong, not only for her but for Talon. She was going through her own issues. She believed in him when he didn't believe in himself... Even when he continued to push her away. She never went far. Something drawing her back in. Something drawing them both together, with chemistry that is off the charts. The push and pull with these two was enough to send me crazy. (In the best way possible of course) She knew there was something different about him, but she had no idea what she was about to find out would change her life completely.<br><br>Will they work whatever it is between them out? Will it be happily ever after for them?<br><br>Book 1 slayed me. absolutely slayed me, it broke me... There were some scenes in this book that were familiar to me, that hit home HARD for me. I'm not going into deep with this review, I could sit and ramble on about it and how amazing it is, or I can tell you to go and grab a copy and give it a good chance. I doubt you'll be disappointed. I believe going in blind is the best thing you can do with this book and series.<br><br>𝗣𝗹𝗲𝗮𝘀𝗲 𝘁𝗮𝗸𝗲 𝗻𝗼𝘁𝗲: 𝗧𝗵𝗶𝘀 𝗶𝘀𝗻'𝘁 𝗳𝗼𝗿 𝘁𝗵𝗲 𝗳𝗮𝗶𝗻𝘁 𝗼𝗳 𝗵𝗲𝗮𝗿𝘁, 𝘁𝗵𝗶𝘀 𝗶𝘀𝗻'𝘁 𝘀𝗼𝗺𝗲 𝗹𝗶𝗴𝗵𝘁 𝗮𝗻𝗱 𝗳𝗹𝘂𝗳𝗳𝘆 𝗿𝗲𝗮𝗱. 𝗜𝘁 𝘁𝗮𝗸𝗲𝘀 𝘀𝗼𝗺𝗲 𝗿𝗲𝗮𝗹-𝗹𝗶𝗳𝗲 𝘁𝗿𝗮𝘂𝗺𝗮 𝗮𝗻𝗱 𝘁𝗵𝗲 𝗮𝘂𝘁𝗵𝗼𝗿 𝗱𝗼𝗲𝘀 𝗻𝗼𝘁 𝘀𝗵𝘆 𝗮𝘄𝗮𝘆 𝗳𝗿𝗼𝗺 𝗺𝘂𝗰𝗵 𝗮𝗻𝗱 𝘀𝗼𝗺𝗲 𝗼𝗳 𝘁𝗵𝗲𝘀𝗲 𝗶𝘀𝘀𝘂𝗲𝘀 𝗮𝗻𝗱 𝘀𝗶𝘁𝘂𝗮𝘁𝗶𝗼𝗻𝘀 𝗰𝗼𝗺𝗲 𝘄𝗶𝘁𝗵 𝘁𝗿𝗶𝗴𝗴𝗲𝗿 𝘄𝗮𝗿𝗻𝗶𝗻𝗴𝘀.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1567925876i/28116871._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></span>

<div id="review_1952718320" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1952718320" />
    <a title="Erin Daniels" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/64221521-erin-daniels"><img alt="Erin Daniels" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1485877620p2/64221521.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1952718320?book_show_action=true">Mar 26, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Erin Daniels" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Erin Daniels" href="/user/show/64221521-erin-daniels">Erin Daniels</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1952718320" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4788699147693723404">How do I describe how bad a book is without sounding like I'm exaggerating? I haven't figured that one out so screw it - here's my review.<br/><br/>This book was hands down one of the worst books I've ever downloaded from Audible in my life. So many of the passages were so horribly written that cringing became a game of diminishing returns and I had to start flinching. I seldom talk back to a recording but this seven hour tour was peppered with so many "wth's" and "are you kidding me's" that it might as w</span>
  <span id="freeText4788699147693723404" style="display:none">How do I describe how bad a book is without sounding like I'm exaggerating? I haven't figured that one out so screw it - here's my review.<br /><br />This book was hands down one of the worst books I've ever downloaded from Audible in my life. So many of the passages were so horribly written that cringing became a game of diminishing returns and I had to start flinching. I seldom talk back to a recording but this seven hour tour was peppered with so many "wth's" and "are you kidding me's" that it might as well have been a duet. <br /><br />First of all Talon Steel? Talon Steel? The nice, down to earth, sane brothers have names like Ryan and Jonas so of course dark and stormy bro has to be named Talon. Because all of this was clear at birth. And of course Broody McDanger was a marine who served in Iraq because troubled. And let's not leave Jade out of the line of fire. Jade has the emotional intelligence of a pack of ramen and is about as deep as the mugs of tea she is constantly making in the microwave. She is only slightly annoyed at being left at the altar after a seven year relationship and she lets her best friend's brother degrade her every chance he gets yet use her for sex after getting something that passes for consent and we're supposed to see her as someone capable of making good choices? <br /><br />And Marjorie can't think her way out of a paper bag. You can't pick your bff up from the airport so who do you send to get her instead? One of your considerate, polite, charming brothers? Lol, where's the fun in that? No, let's send the misanthropic, sexual opportunist with anger management problems instead. Let's send the character who, if this were jane Eyre, would have been locked away in Rochester's attic instead of Bertha. The author clearly didn't know what to do with her so she sleeps a lot. And in case you miss that she and everyone else will repeat it. A lot. But if I had to spend time with Talon and Jade I might stay curled up in my room in the fetal position too.<br /><br />And speaking of repetition you will never be allowed to forget that Talon doesn't want anyone to get close to him because he has walls and no one can break down those walls because those walls are never coming down because walls are meant to keep people out and stuff because walls. It's not that you don't sympathize with him as a reader it's just that you get so few chances to do so because Talon is a first class jerk. I don't mind damaged or troubled but all he's giving me is Blue Steel. By chapter five I'd settle for his Le Tigre look. And Talon constantly lets us know that the countless chicks he's had sex with were so hot for it and he is not rape-y. He is not rape-y nor does he have boundary or permission issues. Are we clear?<br /><br />The kitchen encounters were creepy - even as the reader I wanted to take out a restraining order on Talon. The sex scenes were creepy - this is the first romance I've ever read where I thought both partners needed a ball gag. The post-coital head-tripping wasn't interesting enough to be creepy: If I have sex with her I can finally get her out of my head. Okay, we just had sex and she's, like, totally still in my head and there's the whole walls situation so we better have sex once more and this time it is so going to work. Rinse and repeat...<br /><br />The plot was paper-thin, the characters were unlikable, the dialogue was fifth grade book report hilarious, the setting apparently consisted of the kitchen table, the shower and the echo chamber that was Talon's head-space and the ending was only shocking because I didn't think the book could get any worse. The author threw in a cheap-ass cliffhanger just to remind me that it doesn't pay to dream. <br /><br />I'll never get back those seven hours of my life but if I can save another reader from the fresh hell that was this book then it was worth it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4788699147693723404" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer438580715049944769">'Craving' by Helen Hardt is book One in the "Steel Brothers" Saga. This is the story of Talon and Jade. <br/>There is a cliffhanger to this book so please make note of that. I will say that even though I am not a fan of cliffhangers I understand how much another book was needed when dealing with Talon and Jade's story. In addition, please note I thought this was shadowing on a Dark Romance type theme. Not so much heart and flowers of traditional romances. <br/>Jade is uprooting herself from her hometown a</span>
  <span id="freeText438580715049944769" style="display:none">'Craving' by Helen Hardt is book One in the "Steel Brothers" Saga. This is the story of Talon and Jade. <br />There is a cliffhanger to this book so please make note of that. I will say that even though I am not a fan of cliffhangers I understand how much another book was needed when dealing with Talon and Jade's story. In addition, please note I thought this was shadowing on a Dark Romance type theme. Not so much heart and flowers of traditional romances. <br />Jade is uprooting herself from her hometown after being left at the alter. Her best friend Marjorie talks her into coming to stay with her and look for a job there. So Jade heads out to make a new start!<br />Marjorie’s brother Talon picks her up at the airport. This is the first time Jade has met Talon and she is shocked by her reaction. Jade is quickly hot for him but he is not a talkative person and seems distant. Not like his brothers and sister. <br />Talon too can't believe how much he wants Jade but he has a mind set not to get close to any women...and just take what they willing give. But that is hard to stick to around Jade...but he does tries to keep a distance. <br />It didn't take long to fall in love with this story! <br /> "My honest review is for a special copy I voluntarily read."<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/1831318-sissy-s-romance-book-review-for-you">https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/1...</a> <br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.amazon.com/gp/profile/A2HX0B5ELOPP5Z?ie=UTF8&amp;ref_=sv_ys_3">https://www.amazon.com/gp/profile/A2H...</a><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/RomanceBookReview">https://www.facebook.com/RomanceBookR...</a><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/groups/1709181636033417/">https://www.facebook.com/groups/17091...</a><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://sissymaereads.blogspot.com/">http://sissymaereads.blogspot.com/</a> <br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://romancebookreviewforyou.wordpress.com/">https://romancebookreviewforyou.wordp...</a><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://booklikes.com/blog">http://booklikes.com/blog</a> <br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.tumblr.com/blog/romancebookreviewforyoublog">https://www.tumblr.com/blog/romancebo...</a><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.pinterest.com/u2soapsrus/">https://www.pinterest.com/u2soapsrus/</a><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9345864836561271579">OMG so hot! AND ends on a cliffhanger... UGH<br/>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br/>Sometimes you pick up a book that you know is going to be a winner from the very first page. This book is one of those.<br/><br/>Where to even start? The character of Talon is a deep conflicted hurting man who is desperate for release from his anguish. We get hints along the way of the depths of his issues and the only one that seems to be able to take the edge off is Jade.<br/><br/>Talon is afraid of hur</span>
  <span id="freeText9345864836561271579" style="display:none">OMG so hot! AND ends on a cliffhanger... UGH<br />~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br />Sometimes you pick up a book that you know is going to be a winner from the very first page. This book is one of those.<br /><br />Where to even start? The character of Talon is a deep conflicted hurting man who is desperate for release from his anguish. We get hints along the way of the depths of his issues and the only one that seems to be able to take the edge off is Jade.<br /><br />Talon is afraid of hurting her and does everything he can to push her away. But emotions and feelings run deep.<br /><br />The author crafted a book that gives you a major feels. You hurt when he hurts and your emotions are high and low, just like his.<br /><br />As I got towards the end I kept hoping that we would get an HEA and not a cliffhanger. But I was wrong. Now that I think about it, the author could never of done justice to this man and any kind of relationship without an in-depth story that I just know will rip out guts out.<br /><br />This author has created a masterpiece with her emotionally charged story and series. High sexual tension and amazing scenes of passion are off the charts. I cannot wait to dive into book two and three. This author has completely sucked me in.<br /><br /></span>

  <span id="freeText2992373805413649924" style="display:none">Craving <br />Steel Brothers #1 <br />Helen Hardt<br />5⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br /><br />Excellent story!! Loved this one from the beginning to the end. And of course it left me craving for more. Can’t wait to read the next book in this series. <br /><br />After being left at the altar, Jade Roberts seeks solace at her best friend’s ranch on the Colorado western slope. Her humiliation still ripe, she doesn't expect to be attracted to her friend’s reticent brother, but when the gorgeous cowboy kisses her, all bets are off.<br /><br />Talon Steel is broken. Having never fully healed from a horrific childhood trauma, he simply exists, taking from women what is offered and giving nothing in return...until Jade Roberts catapults into his life. She is beautiful, sweet, and giving, and his desire for her becomes a craving he fears he'll never be able to satisfy.<br /><br />Passion sizzles between the two lovers...but long-buried secrets haunt them both and may eventually tear them apart.<br /><br /><br />This author did an amazing job writing this story. It has so much love and angst and all the other feelings all wrapped up in one story. <br />Thanks NetGalley for the arc in exchange for my honest review.<br /></span>

        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/30239118-craving">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=family-series">family-series</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1781830401" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer7117433846146488126">I found this read through an ad on FB, and it basically stated that this was a series to read after Fifty Shades. I'll admit, I am one of those people that really enjoyed the Fifty Shades trilogy (I won't even discuss the book that came after the trilogy..cough...cough..."Grey" ) Anyway, I was excited to see that maybe this would be just as good; if not better...I have to be honest and say that this was just an ok read for me. It had great potential, and I am going to remain positive and hope th</span>
  <span id="freeText7117433846146488126" style="display:none">I found this read through an ad on FB, and it basically stated that this was a series to read after Fifty Shades. I'll admit, I am one of those people that really enjoyed the Fifty Shades trilogy (I won't even discuss the book that came after the trilogy..cough...cough..."Grey" ) Anyway, I was excited to see that maybe this would be just as good; if not better...I have to be honest and say that this was just an ok read for me. It had great potential, and I am going to remain positive and hope that as the story progresses, it might fall into place...but as for book one...I was disappointed, yet intrigued to the point where I will carry on. My biggest complaint was that it was hard to connect to the main characters. Considering Talon was dealing with a crap ton of trauma from his childhood, I had a hard time empathising with him. He was an ass for the most part, and I would have liked to have seen him have a soft side to him somewhere. Maybe that will still come in the second book...I sure hope so. Then there is Jade, I found her to be a bit of a door mat at times, then she would change to a bitch...she had quite a bipolar feel to her at times!!! The sex between these two was hot...but forewarning....there is a ton of it! In fact, I'd say they spent most of their times in the sack or shower, rather than discussing what their relationship meant...Again, let's hope there is more communication in book two~! <br /><br />The story starts with Jade making a move to her friends ranch in Colorado after she has been left at the alter by her husband to be. Her friend lives on a huge ranch with her brothers, and has welcomed Jade to come stay. The Steel siblings are very rich, and have split ownership of the Ranch. Talon Steel is the middle brother, and he is the mysterious and dark one. He has a ton of trauma and secrets, and is not the type to open up to anyone. When he gets a look at his sister's friend, he knows there is something different about his attraction to her. He doesn't like it, and immediately he erects his walls up very high. During their many midnight meetings in the kitchen when Jade and Talon can't sleep, sparks begin to fly, and both their lives will never be the same when the walls start crumbling down.<br /><br />I am very hopeful for this series. I think it has a ton of potential, and because of this I will continue on for now. My fingers are crossed that things will pick up. It isn't the most original book out there, but it still has the sexy brooding heroes that we come to love in our romances!! Let's hope Talon will get through his many issues, and become the hero I swoon for!!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="7117433846146488126" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1837551304" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1837551304" />
    <a title="Lissa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30936578-lissa"><img alt="Lissa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605458219p2/30936578.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1837551304?book_show_action=true">Dec 12, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lissa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lissa" href="/user/show/30936578-lissa">Lissa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781943893171" href="/book/show/27819474-craving">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30936578-lissa?shelf=could-have-been-so-much-better">could-have-been-so-much-better</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30936578-lissa?shelf=ebook">ebook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30936578-lissa?shelf=consent-issues">consent-issues</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30936578-lissa?shelf=dont-understand-the-hype">dont-understand-the-hype</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30936578-lissa?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30936578-lissa?shelf=fucked-up-main-character">fucked-up-main-character</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30936578-lissa?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30936578-lissa?shelf=excuse-me-while-i-rage">excuse-me-while-i-rage</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30936578-lissa?shelf=abused-hero">abused-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30936578-lissa?shelf=sexually-abused-main-character">sexually-abused-main-character</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1837551304" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16938151996857072993">Have you ever agreed to buddy read a trilogy (which I just discovered has now morphed into at least a six book series) with a friend who swears up and down that you will absolutely <i>love</i> a book, and then you get halfway through said book and you are about to beat your head against the wall and wonder why in the hell you ever agreed to buddy read this?<br/><br/>Please tell me I'm not the only one to make this mistake.<br/><br/>And I can't really blame my friend, because she does know that I love messed up books (the </span>
  <span id="freeText16938151996857072993" style="display:none">Have you ever agreed to buddy read a trilogy (which I just discovered has now morphed into at least a six book series) with a friend who swears up and down that you will absolutely <i>love</i> a book, and then you get halfway through said book and you are about to beat your head against the wall and wonder why in the hell you ever agreed to buddy read this?<br /><br />Please tell me I'm not the only one to make this mistake.<br /><br />And I can't really blame my friend, because she does know that I love messed up books (the more messed up, the better - usually), and the book is set on the western slope of Colorado, an area of the state for which I will always hold a fondness. So my friend really did think that I would love these books. <br /><br />First off, the author gets several things wrong about the setting. Granted, I know that "Snow Creek" is a made-up town, so I can't fault her for anything there. But she does use Grand Junction as a backdrop for the first few chapters, and it pops up every so often, and there are just things <i>wrong</i> about Junction. Spoiler cut just because I'm probably about to go on a rant here.<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[First off, I have never heard a local say "I am going to Grand Junction." The city is nearly always referred to as just plain Junction by anyone who lives close by, and I can always point out the n00bs who refer to Junction as anything other than, well, Junction. And the airplane flying into the airport - at least three seats across before an aisle? I have a hard time believing any flight into Junction would be a 2-3 or a 3-3. Usually it's a puddlejumper 1-2; rarely I have seen a 2-2, but never anything bigger than a 2-2. Also, Talon, when he picks Jade up at the airport, states that he is "parked on this level," or the level of the baggage claim. Yeah, no fucking shit. There's only one "level" at the Junction airport - it's called a big parking lot outside, where your car sits in the desert sun with no protection and they rip you off for $10 a day. There are no parking garages and no "levels." All of this may seem petty to criticize, and perhaps it is, but I am very familiar with Junction - just imagine if someone set a book in your hometown and got ALL THE THINGS wrong. It's annoying to me. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />But, okay, let's give the author a little leeway here. And let's judge the story on its merits and not the glaring factual errors that bug the ever living shit out of me and my OCD.<br /><br />Talon is all sorts of messed up, which I usually like, but he is such a fucking asshole to Jade that I can't handle him. He totally dismisses any pain she feels about being stood up at the altar in front of all of her friends and family because it doesn't match his ~*~pain~*~ that she doesn't even know about and is a total ass about the whole thing. And, granted, his past is horrible, but that doesn't make the fact that she was humiliated any less painful to her, especially since she doesn't know anything about Talon's past except that he was in the Marines for the while. <br /><br />Talon was abused; that much is made pretty clear, and the extent of his abuse is revealed as the book progresses. But he pushes hard against Jade's boundaries and does not take no for an answer. There is more than one instance in this book where Jade is not exactly into having sex with Talon, but he doesn't listen to her protests and eventually "convinces" her to go along with him, which she does in almost every instance. No. That's rapey as hell and incredibly not kosher, not heroic, and not acceptable. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[There's an instance when they are in a public place and he wants to have sex with her in a public place, which she is totally not feeling at all, and he keeps pushing until she literally has to force him to back the fuck up before he rapes her. Oooh, so sexy. And yes, I know that adults who have survived childhood sexual abuse can have problems with understanding boundaries and etc, but Talon pushes that envelope way, way past the line of "this is acceptable" and doesn't seem to understand that at all; nor does he seem willing to examine his own behavior to see why she feels that is unacceptable. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Also, the sex scenes are just...so awful. The description of Jade's anatomy is hilariously bad, to the point that I was attempting not to laugh when the author went on and on about Jade's "red" labia (sounds like there's some serious chafing going on, which I wouldn't be surprised about, considering how much "shoving" organs into orifices occurs in this book). And Talon was "abrading the anterior of [her] pussy [with his fingers]" at one point (that is a direct quote). Let me say as a lesbian - fucking OUCH, use some lube or do some foreplay to get her wet or something! Someone abrading any part of my anatomy does <i>not</i> sound like a good time.<br /><br />There's quite a bit of instalove - they have a lot of (horribly written) sex, but there doesn't seem to be anything between them except some chemistry. And Talon waxes hot and cold when it comes to Jade - he can't stop craving her, and then he's pushing her away. Once again, I can understand this as a sexual assault victim, but jesus, it got so fucking annoying watching him whipsaw back and forth like that. <br /><br />Some of the descriptions seemed just...odd, as well (besides Jade's "red" labia). Talon compares her gray eyes to "tanzanite," which seems way left field to me. That's a deep blue, by the way, because I had no idea what the fuck it was - and definitely nowhere close to Jade's self-described "gray" eyes. And listening to Talon talk to his brothers comes across as very odd, stilted, and not realistic at all.<br /><br />Well, the one thing I can say is that I totally agree with the author - there's no better peaches in the world than western slope peaches. <br /><br />The thing is, I think that this book really had some potential, because there is an intriguing mystery going on with the Steel family. But it takes a backseat to all of the awkward sex and ridiculous drama. It's disappointing, but apparently unless I find an excellent excuse, I am stuck reading the next two books in the series. Sigh. </span>
  <a data-text-id="16938151996857072993" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        rated it

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6844907-jessica?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6844907-jessica?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6844907-jessica?shelf=call-a-doctor-my-ovaries-exploded">call-a-doctor-my-ovaries-exploded</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1641038921" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2754659348589184397">Jesus. This is one of those books that leaves you in a fog after you're done. I need to get to the conclusion and have Talon finally be at peace. I definitely didn't know that this was a cliffhanger. I'd just seen it, randomly decided to read it and was sucked in. It's so well written, I was essentially forced to read it in one sitting. Now I have to pray that the next one's already been published. If not, I'll just keep sitting here in my book haze.</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1692820841" />
    <a title="Ro" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8158262-ro"><img alt="Ro" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1581293246p2/8158262.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1692820841?book_show_action=true">Jul 09, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ro" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ro" href="/user/show/8158262-ro">Ro</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781943893171" href="/book/show/27819474-craving">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1692820841" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3194708018562368992">The story is great. The writing not so much. Author used such repetitive phrasing I became annoyed halfway through. It's like she didn't know any other way to describe anything. <br/><br/>What I disliked most is that there seemed to be no buildup. I know this is a story but everything just happened so fast it was just ridiculous. <br/><br/>Jade is left at the altar, literally, and it was like she hardly cared. Oh yeah, she knew that maybe she wasn't as in love as she thought but she hardly gives the whole thing a s</span>
  <span id="freeText3194708018562368992" style="display:none">The story is great. The writing not so much. Author used such repetitive phrasing I became annoyed halfway through. It's like she didn't know any other way to describe anything. <br /><br />What I disliked most is that there seemed to be no buildup. I know this is a story but everything just happened so fast it was just ridiculous. <br /><br />Jade is left at the altar, literally, and it was like she hardly cared. Oh yeah, she knew that maybe she wasn't as in love as she thought but she hardly gives the whole thing a second thought. Then she's sleeping with Talon. That's actually a little believable. Stranger things have happened, I guess. <br /><br />But she's on the ranch two days and already digging into his brothers on his background. The one brother never even saw the two interact and he's like, "there's something special," but the sister who has seen them together doesn't have anything to say. In fact, I think the book ends without her having any clue her best friend and brother are sleeping together. <br /><br />Talon is mentally distraught from a childhood tragedy, and I like the tortured hero angle, but it all seemed contrived. I'm supposed to feel sorry for him and want to heal all his wounds but I was a little confused as to why I should care. Jade seemed whiny at times. There was very little depth to the characters. <br /><br />I did very much enjoy the undercurrent of the family drama. I'd like to know more but I doubt I will seek out the rest of the series. I didn't like how the book ended on a total cliffhanger. I expected Jade and Talon to fairly resolve their issues, then book two would move on to one of the other brothers or Marj. Guess not. <br /><br />This is decent enough for a long flight or the long wait at the dentist office. It wasn't completely horrible but it's certainly not something I'm anxious for the next instalment. </span>
  <a data-text-id="3194708018562368992" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2191106187?book_show_action=true">Nov 21, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shel" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shel" href="/user/show/25947984-shel">Shel</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Adult readers</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Shel by: </span>
      Meredith Wild, Martha Frantz and Helen Hardt
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2191106187" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6795841608741340135">Craving is an intense drama/romance. This story is not for all but it pulled me in and kept me enthralled. Talon is fighting demons within himself that he has dealt with since he was 10 years old. Nightmares no one should have to face or live through. His brothers Jonas and Ryan are dealing with guilt from the experience Talon went through, each in their own way. Marjorie their sister and the youngest of the Steel's knows nothing of her brothers' pains and guilt. Jade, Marjorie's long time frien</span>
  <span id="freeText6795841608741340135" style="display:none">Craving is an intense drama/romance. This story is not for all but it pulled me in and kept me enthralled. Talon is fighting demons within himself that he has dealt with since he was 10 years old. Nightmares no one should have to face or live through. His brothers Jonas and Ryan are dealing with guilt from the experience Talon went through, each in their own way. Marjorie their sister and the youngest of the Steel's knows nothing of her brothers' pains and guilt. Jade, Marjorie's long time friend comes to stay with her and becomes involved in this family and with Talon in ways she never imagined. Craving is dark, dramatic and oh so sexy. It has a mystery you will follow through all nine books to find the puzzle pieces and solve the reasons for the Steel siblings torment. You will not be sorry for stating or finishing this series. Helen Hardt keeps you turning the pages.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer344915957798574861">DNF @ 52%<br/><br/>Craving is the first book in the Steel Brothers Saga and follows a woman called Jade who ends up being dumped at the alter on her wedding day and moving to a ranch which is owned by her best friend. There, she meets the Steel brothers with one of them called Talon becoming instantly attracted towards her. The novel follows their relationship as well as their struggles with personal issues and feelings that they've kept hidden away from others. I purchased this on a whim during a free Ki</span>
  <span id="freeText344915957798574861" style="display:none">DNF @ 52%<br /><br />Craving is the first book in the Steel Brothers Saga and follows a woman called Jade who ends up being dumped at the alter on her wedding day and moving to a ranch which is owned by her best friend. There, she meets the Steel brothers with one of them called Talon becoming instantly attracted towards her. The novel follows their relationship as well as their struggles with personal issues and feelings that they've kept hidden away from others. I purchased this on a whim during a free Kindle Books search but didn't realise how erotic the plot would be. It was a struggle to keep my interest strong and after the halfway mark, I simply decided that Craving was not for me. The sex scenes were graphic and the insta-love I found uncomfortable. I will not be continuing with the series. </span>

  <span id="freeText95988566288383167" style="display:none">This is an emotional roller coaster that I could not get off. <br /><br />This is an epic story about two broken souls that try to heal one another. I read this book in two days. I could not put it down. I can not wait for the next book of this emotional love story. <br /><br />The two main characters are Jade and Talon. Jade was left at the alter on her wedding day. In order to try to start an new beginning she moves in with her best friend at the Steele brothers ranch. Jade grew up with all the brother except one Talon. They feel the chemistry between them as soon as they meet in the airport. <br /><br />Talon served in the military which still haunts him. We also find out he also suffers from a childhood trauma which he relives every night. His escape is to the best in the bedroom. He knows he has some type of feelings for Jade but he does not know if it is love. Will they break each other's walls down and find the love that they both want? I surly hope so. </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781943893171" href="/book/show/27819474-craving">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41806030-erin?shelf=ugh">ugh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41806030-erin?shelf=not-for-me">not-for-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41806030-erin?shelf=read-2017">read-2017</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1933993353" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8579387622039028347">In this book the love interest, Talon Steel, almost rapes the main character twice. At least. And the book seems really determined to make you believe that this is all "swoon worthy" and "romantic" but it's not. Rape will never ever <b>EVER</b> be romantic. It doesn't matter that Talon felt kind of sorry afterwards. IT DOESN'T MATTER HOW HE FELT AFTER THE FACT.<br/><br/>Besides the almost rape, the relationship between Talon and Jade is just straight up abusive. I don't care that he suffered a horrific childhood</span>
  <span id="freeText8579387622039028347" style="display:none">In this book the love interest, Talon Steel, almost rapes the main character twice. At least. And the book seems really determined to make you believe that this is all "swoon worthy" and "romantic" but it's not. Rape will never ever <b>EVER</b> be romantic. It doesn't matter that Talon felt kind of sorry afterwards. IT DOESN'T MATTER HOW HE FELT AFTER THE FACT.<br /><br />Besides the almost rape, the relationship between Talon and Jade is just straight up abusive. I don't care that he suffered a horrific childhood trauma. That does not excuse him for his actions throughout this book. He screams at her, belittles her, at one point grabs her hard enough to bruise her (in response Jade claims that it's fine because she loves him which is plain MESSED UP), and in general relentlessly just treats her like shit. The ONLY time he's kinda nice to her is when they're having sex and I'm just??????????????????????????????????????<br /><br />I could go on for a really long time about how much this book bothered me (TALON STEEL??? WTH KINDA NAME IS THAT ANY WAY), but I think I'm just going to cut it short now in order to spare my sanity. Instead, I'm going to end with a plea to New Adult authors in general: <b> Please, please STOP romanticizing rape and abuse. It makes impressionable readers believe this is okay and normal in relationships. Please stop contributing to that culture.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="8579387622039028347" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1920599328" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15842766787654724805">Title: Craving<br/>Author: Helen Hardt<br/>Publisher: Waterhouse Press<br/>Series: Steel Brother Saga # 1<br/>Reviewed By: Arlena Dean<br/>Rating: Five<br/>Review:<br/><br/>"Craving" by Helen Hardt<br/><br/>My Thoughts....<br/><br/>Interesting series 'Steel Brothers Saga # 1' that features Talon Steel and Jade Roberts who were definitely two broken souls. This author gives the reader quite a good story and be warned it end on a cliffhanger where you will have to get the rest of the story in later series. Be ready for quite a emotional roller coaster ride</span>
  <span id="freeText15842766787654724805" style="display:none">Title: Craving<br />Author: Helen Hardt<br />Publisher: Waterhouse Press<br />Series: Steel Brother Saga # 1<br />Reviewed By: Arlena Dean<br />Rating: Five<br />Review:<br /><br />"Craving" by Helen Hardt<br /><br />My Thoughts....<br /><br />Interesting series 'Steel Brothers Saga # 1' that features Talon Steel and Jade Roberts who were definitely two broken souls. This author gives the reader quite a good story and be warned it end on a cliffhanger where you will have to get the rest of the story in later series. Be ready for quite a emotional roller coaster ride and lots of twist and turns for these two. The main question is will they be able to heal each other? <br /><br />After Jade is left at the alter on her wedding day she goes to stay with her friend, Marjorie Steel<br />at the Steele brothers ranch while she is waiting to get her results from the bar exam to become a lawyer. What will happen after Jade meets Talon Steele? Will it be something their for them especially for Talon at the first sight of her[picking her up from the airport? But as we read their is a lots that had gone on with Talon not only was he returning from the Marines but something had happen to Talon in his past during his childhood. What was Talon's childhood secret that it seemed that he was always struggling so hard with especially when he was with Jade? And then their was the question to what was it between Jade and Talon as it seems that he simply craved her..all the time? Why was it so hard for Talon to open up about what had gone on with him especially to Jade. Will he seek help? This is a very mature adult read so be aware that this story is loaded with a lots of erotica sex that will be all over the place for these two. Well, to get all of these questions answered and so much more you will have to pick up "Craving" to see just how well this author brings it out to the reader. It will be one heck of a good read. <br /><br />So, I guess the reader will have to get the next series to see if these two finally get their HEA.</span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21404261-sara-kate?shelf=netgalley-books">netgalley-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1809276389" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8298630271831998578">Wow...so first if all let me just say how Yummy Talon is! Phew. The scenes between him and Jade were hot! I'm sucker for a tortured bad boy. Boy, Talon sure is a tortured soul. Right away I was intrigued by his mysterious brooding self. I thought it had something to do with his time spent in the military and he is suffering from PTSD which is why he can't sleep and spends the late hours of the night in the kitchen with a glass of water staring off until Jade moves into the Steel Ranch after her </span>
  <span id="freeText8298630271831998578" style="display:none">Wow...so first if all let me just say how Yummy Talon is! Phew. The scenes between him and Jade were hot! I'm sucker for a tortured bad boy. Boy, Talon sure is a tortured soul. Right away I was intrigued by his mysterious brooding self. I thought it had something to do with his time spent in the military and he is suffering from PTSD which is why he can't sleep and spends the late hours of the night in the kitchen with a glass of water staring off until Jade moves into the Steel Ranch after her ex-fiancé leaves her at the alter. Jade finds herself restless after her ordeal and goes to Mae herself a late night cup of tea where she finds Talon sitting at the counter. This is where ther "relationship" grows and things start to develop. Jade seems to chip some of ice away from Talon and tries to help him. They have explosive chemistry from the start and Talon starts to wish for something more than what he thinks he can have. <br><br>The bomb with Talon toward the end broke my heart. I'm curious to see what or if Jade will find anything or figure out what happened to them. There are still a lot of questions unanswered but I'm sure that it the author's way to keep you interested! This was a great start to the series and I will be confusing this series for sure. I need to know what is going to happen with Talon and Jade.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1481574172i/21434034.png" width="80" height="80" alt="Professional Reader" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17901527374020808312">Oh my goodness this book was so so good! I read in one sitting. I absolutely could not put it down!<br/>After being left at the alter by the man she has spent years planning a future with, Jade Roberts moves in with her best friend Marj at Marj's family's ranch. She is there to wait for healing and her Bar exam results. <br/>Talon Steel is the on brother that Jade hasn't met, so she is suprised to find the very sexy man waiting to pick her up at the airport. There is an instant attraction and chemisty bet</span>
  <span id="freeText17901527374020808312" style="display:none">Oh my goodness this book was so so good! I read in one sitting. I absolutely could not put it down!<br />After being left at the alter by the man she has spent years planning a future with, Jade Roberts moves in with her best friend Marj at Marj's family's ranch. She is there to wait for healing and her Bar exam results. <br />Talon Steel is the on brother that Jade hasn't met, so she is suprised to find the very sexy man waiting to pick her up at the airport. There is an instant attraction and chemisty between these two immediately. <br />Talon has suffered tremendously as a child yet everyone is very quite about it. Talon is just trying to get through lift the only way he knows how, one day at a time, and shut off all emotion. and never ever let anyone in. <br />Will these two stop fighting what is between them, move past the hurt and anger of the past, and find solace in eachother? I cannot wait for the next book to find out!<br />This was my first read by Helen but it will not be my last. I really hope she writes fast, as I am chomping at the bit for more!!!!!</span>

<div id="review_1630244939" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1630244939" />
    <a title="The BookChick " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6190526-the-bookchick"><img alt="The BookChick " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1546023730p2/6190526.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1630244939?book_show_action=true">May 05, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="The BookChick " class="user" itemprop="url" name="The BookChick " href="/user/show/6190526-the-bookchick">The BookChick </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781943893171" href="/book/show/27819474-craving">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6190526-the-bookchick?shelf=00-2016-read">00-2016-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6190526-the-bookchick?shelf=3-star-read">3-star-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6190526-the-bookchick?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6190526-the-bookchick?shelf=erotic-romance-or-erotic-elements">erotic-romance-or-erotic-elements</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6190526-the-bookchick?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6190526-the-bookchick?shelf=damaged-protagonist-s">damaged-protagonist-s</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6190526-the-bookchick?shelf=cliffy">cliffy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6190526-the-bookchick?shelf=dark-romance">dark-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1630244939" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14905739555229248562">This is my first book by Helen Hardt, and sadly I didn't love it. Don't get me wrong, I did not hate it either. I'm just...neutral about it. I never felt an emotional connection between Talon and Jade beyond their fiery physical connection. The story certainly did not make me lose myself in it. Im not sure why exactly but I will attribute specifically to the pacing of the story. I felt as if parts of it lagged; but, that could be because Craving is first book in the series and a good deal of wor</span>
  <span id="freeText14905739555229248562" style="display:none">This is my first book by Helen Hardt, and sadly I didn't love it. Don't get me wrong, I did not hate it either. I'm just...neutral about it. I never felt an emotional connection between Talon and Jade beyond their fiery physical connection. The story certainly did not make me lose myself in it. Im not sure why exactly but I will attribute specifically to the pacing of the story. I felt as if parts of it lagged; but, that could be because Craving is first book in the series and a good deal of world building has to occur in the first book which sometimes creates a disconnect between reader and story. Unfortunately, that is what happened to me in this story. I listened to the story in audio format and I enjoyed the narration which helped to bridge some of the story disconnect. All that said, I'm intrigued about the Marge story angle and curious to uncover what really happened to Talon; therefore, I'll be on the look out for the next installment in the series.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14905739555229248562" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ZKcJgfv/GOT97DEI2mLetyZOtrw2Eu5U3xDSm7yBA7SizryETGzb5zpCmJrrGWweQeEt9xUo9F20Lm4NzT4mUg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('RhQwGO4Otxkxusr0GnT+W9BmSadWvkV+Z2xywwBQBLGAfYUdWZ10GvYUY2YrD0zyt8nS7HWEX3cMUs5Vce8hVw==')})
  }

        $('bookCover_25655922').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('bookCover_25655922').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('bookCover_25655922').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
